< text>
Do not let the placement of this place throw you off from quality. Set in a mall food court, this place tops Gaby's and other Mediterranean restaurants near by.

You can order a whole grilled mackerel.

Their salmon falls apart as you bite into it. My mouth was in shock as I am used to tough salmon from kebab houses.

Got the Greek salad, delicious if you like tang and zest as their dressing is has a. delightful light balsamic taste with added blended olives.

Prepare to wait about 15 minutes for your food. Each dish is prepared with each order. The meat is grilled fresh where you can see it.

Take home spices and hot sauces available.< /text>

< text>
Two things I love... tangy and spicy. One other that I‚Äôve recently added: healthy. Ive been doing my best to avoid the typical junk that I put in my body so I tried something a little different. This place is pretty good. The menu pictures will make your mouth water. A lot to choose from. The salad bar looked so so but the tomato and cucumber salad was delicious! One bite and I was in love. I would‚Äôve bought a whole container of it! Very light and refreshing taste. The chicken kabob that I ordered was tasty. Nothing to die for. The taste of charbroiled chicken with a bit of lemony flavor. The rice also had a bit of a tangy zest to it. The roasted tomato that it was paired with in addition to the pita slices was a good offset and/or balance. Overall I recommend trying it. Only minus one star because while I was waiting, one of the servers had a disagreement with a customer and started back and forth. The customer said she preferred salad instead of rice and the server insisted that she should have asked before hand. The customer said she shops here all the time and always does ask before hand but that it must not have been communicated. Even though the customer was a bit snappy in my opinion, being a customer service rep myself, I would never go back and forth with a customer. Wrong or not, you ave to hold your composure and diffuse the situation in the most cordial manner possible, particularly when other customers are watching. The server definitely popped an attitude and gave some smart remarks when she could have smiled, said ‚ÄúI‚Äôll take care of you‚Äù, and asked that the customer could just make sure the order taker heard her clearly so that they could make sure to have her order perfect next time and ‚Äúthank you‚Äù.<//text>

<user>114861004532389296064</user><name>Jason Harrold< /name><date>1568056567412<//date><Rating>2</Rating>< review>
I came in on Friday and decided to go with the chicken salad with a side of hummus.  I would say that for what I got, the cost is moderately priced.  Not overly expensive but not economical either.
The lettuce was pretty bland, definitely not enough dressing to really flavor the dish. The chicken was good though.  Hummus was ok.  The pita was pretty stiff. If anything I would suggest heating up the pita or making it fresh for the guests and adding additional items to the salad to make it interesting. There were some tomatoes, olives etc but the salad seem to be just thrown together with out any sort of real interest.
Service was unfriendly and the order took a long time.
On a plus side they give you a order device that vibrates when your order is ready.  It took about 20 minutes for a chicken salad with one person in front of me and they didnt seem too busy but thats an outsider prospective.<//review>

<Review>I've had multiple visits to loved ones (maternity, telemetry, CCU, ICU) at this hospital as I grew up in Santa Maria and it's the only game in town. The facility has undergone a major renovation and looks absolutely beautiful, they have a decent cafeteria, family waiting rooms are comfortable, all equipment is new and cutting edge. The staff and volunteers are overwhelming kind and professional though there are a few bad seeds and your experience will likely vary depending on who takes care of you during your stay. The best advice I can give you is to keep on top of your loved ones medications, needs, and plans for discharge/transfer. This is the most challenging part of being in a hospital and while they are supposed to coordinate all the different care being provided on your behalf I found a daily need to advocate for my loved one. Don't assume it is being taken care of, ask lots of questions and make sure you are getting the best care possible.<//Review>< pics>

I went there on Saint Patrick's Day with some friends. I had my first White Russian there, and the old lady behind the bar was an awesome bartender. The decor of the place is very old-timey. Lots of animal heads mounted on the walls, vintage firearms and bayonets and old WWI propaganda recruiting posters and old signs. Overall cozy place, but very small little nook in the street.</Review>

Yay for the Truck Stop! It's close by to work so I can always drop by during lunch. The only downside is that there is only room for three trucks in the little alley and the lunch rush can garner long lines. The Truck Stops has rotating trucks and it's convenient as they post a schedule on their site. I'm a fan of The Chairman and the Little Green Cylco. Their foods never fail to disappoint and always taste fresh and delicious.  Also, it's in a nice little location as you can buy your lunch from the trucks and eat in the areas of seats and tables nearby.</Review>

< review>
For me, this restaurant did not live up to the Google Rating some others have given it. Let's start with its physical presence: It is located in a minor strip mall, it has inadequate parking, it has generic interior appointments, and is quite small. Next, the food: The Enchiladas del Chili Colorado used shredded beef instead of chunks, had no Colorado Sauce inside, very little outside, and were served in quite skimpy portions. Also, the rice (plain and uninspiring) came five minutes after the meal was served. (How could a Mexican Restaurant run out of rice in the middle of the afternoon?) Next, the service: Over the course of our meal, we were served by three different waitresses, none of whom knew what the others had done. The waitress who took our order had an almost incomprehensible Spanish accent. And we had to ask three times to get our check delivered. Next, the drinks: My two Arnold Palmers had inconsistent portions of tea & lemonade and my companion said his Margarita had very little actual tequila in it. Finally, the cost: The food and service were mediocre but the prices were high -- out of line for what we got. I will not return to this restaurant and I recommend others avoid it, as well.<//review>

<username>Steven Lockwood<//username>< rate>

< Review>
This place is sensational! We were greeted very warmly and seated right away. Decent pricing to start off with. Our waitress was nice and accommodating. My friend had never tried horchata before, and theirs was phenomenal. They brought out chips and salsa, and it was excellent, both very fresh and pleasing. I had a burrito enchilada style with green sauce. It was very succulent and moist, and stuffed just right. My friend had the carne asada, which was awesome too (I tried a bite!). His came with a side of refried beans and some tortillas that were obviously homemade. The best part was everything was not smothered in cheese. A lot of Mexican restaurants compensate their bland offerings by loading on the cheese and sauces. This place does not. We will definitely be back here. In a sea of so-so Mexican food, this place rises above.</Review>
